-- Update property average_rating / total_reviews to stay consistent with reviews
UPDATE `properties` p SET `total_reviews` = (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM `property_reviews` r WHERE r.property_id = p.id AND r.status='approved'), `average_rating` = COALESCE((SELECT ROUND(AVG(r.rating),2) FROM `property_reviews` r WHERE r.property_id = p.id AND r.status='approved'), 0.00) WHERE p.id >= 9;
